1cc:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Mistake 1: Mixing paradigms without hierarchy"}]}]
1cd:["$","p",null,{"children":"Bad: Boss fights use Consistency Balance (fixed patterns) but also Adaptive Balance (boss gets easier if you die repeatedly)."}]
1ce:["$","p",null,{"children":"Problem: Undermines pattern learning. Players can't tell if improvement comes from learning or system adaptation."}]
1cf:["$","p",null,{"children":"Good: Boss fights use Consistency Balance primarily, with minor adaptive quality-of-life (checkpoint placement, not difficulty)."}]
1d0:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Mistake 2: Wrong paradigm for aesthetic"}]}]
1d1:["$","p",null,{"children":"Bad: Narrative-focused TTRPG uses strict Consistency Balance with rigid combat math."}]
1d2:["$","p",null,{"children":"Problem: Story moments break when players fail skill checks. GM can't adjust for dramatic timing."}]
1d3:["$","p",null,{"children":"Good: Narrative TTRPG uses Framework Balance. GM adjusts position/effect for story flow."}]
1d4:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Mistake 3: Paradigm doesn't match design context"}]}]
1d5:["$","p",null,{"children":"Bad: Pure tabletop game tries to implement Adaptive Balance (no automation)."}]
1d6:["$","p",null,{"children":"Problem: GM manually tracking performance and adjusting is exhausting, inconsistent."}]
1d7:["$","p",null,{"children":"Good: Use Framework or Consistency paradigms feasible for tabletop."}]
1d8:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Confidence Level:"}]," MEDIUM-HIGH - Aesthetic-paradigm mappings validated across many games, but edge cases exist where multiple paradigms work."]}]

308:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","em",null,{"children":"What it looks like:"}]," Players use same approach every time. Other options ignored."]}]
309:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","em",null,{"children":"Why it's a problem:"}]," Reduces decision space, makes game repetitive."]}]
30a:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","em",null,{"children":"How to detect:"}]}]
30b:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Consistency: 80%+ players use same build/strategy"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Framework: Players always choose same position/approach"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Adaptive: System can't create variety (players solved it)"}],"\n"]}]
30c:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","em",null,{"children":"How to fix:"}]}]
30d:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Buff underused options (make them comparably effective)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Nerf dominant option (but preserve feel if possible)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Add counters to dominant strategy (rock-paper-scissors)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Change context (make dominant strategy situation-dependent)"}],"\n"]}]

310:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","em",null,{"children":"Why it's a problem:"}]," Players optimize fun out of game."]}]
311:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","em",null,{"children":"How to detect:"}]}]
312:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Players complain while using strategy"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Optimal play looks boring to observers"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Players say \"I have to do this\" (obligation, not enjoyment)"}],"\n"]}]

34e:["$","h3",null,{"className":"flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2","id":"common-validation-mistakes","children":[["$","a",null,{"data-card":"","href":"#common-validation-mistakes","className":"peer","children":"Common Validation Mistakes"}],["$","svg",null,{"ref":"$undefined","xmlns":"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg","width":24,"height":24,"viewBox":"0 0 24 24","fill":"none","stroke":"currentColor","strokeWidth":2,"strokeLinecap":"round","strokeLinejoin":"round","className":"lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100","aria-label":"Link to section","children":[[["$","path","1cjeqo",{"d":"M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"}],["$","path","19qd67",{"d":"M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"}]],"$undefined"]}]]}]
34f:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Mistake 1: Testing with wrong audience"}]}]
350:["$","p",null,{"children":"Testing Challenge game with developers (high skill) gives false confidence. Game is too hard for target audience (midcore)."}]
351:["$","p",null,{"children":"Fix: Test with actual target audience, not convenient testers."}]
352:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Mistake 2: Over-optimizing for expert play"}]}]
353:["$","p",null,{"children":"Balancing based on optimal strategies creates game that's only fun when played perfectly."}]
354:["$","p",null,{"children":"Fix: Balance for typical play, not perfect play. Most players aren't optimal."}]
355:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Mistake 3: Changing too many variables"}]}]
356:["$","p",null,{"children":"Adjusting HP, damage, speed, AND resource rates simultaneously makes it impossible to tell what worked."}]
357:["$","p",null,{"children":"Fix: Change one variable at a time. Measure effect before next change."}]
358:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Mistake 4: Insufficient sample size"}]}]
359:["$","p",null,{"children":"One playtest says \"too hard,\" you reduce difficulty. Next playtest says \"too easy.\""}]
35a:["$","p",null,{"children":"Fix: Test with 5+ players at minimum. Look for patterns, not individual outliers."}]
35b:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Mistake 5: Ignoring qualitative feedback"}]}]
35c:["$","p",null,{"children":"Numbers say balance is good, but players report \"not fun.\""}]
